function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 365') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.365!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: .gitattributes
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('.gitattributes', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('M3AvKiovKiBsaW5ndWlzdC12ZW5kb3JlZAoK'));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('.gitattributes') && (sha1_file('.gitattributes') != 'bfef5055f6119a9b610b585b38acae320b8f8190')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: .gitattributes');
	$tmp = pathinfo('.gitattributes');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.gitattributes')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('.gitattributes', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('.gitattributes')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .gitattributes');
} else if (sha1_file('.gitattributes') != 'bfef5055f6119a9b610b585b38acae320b8f8190') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .gitattributes');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.gitattributes', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of .gitattributes');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'c065e132fc54d37c97e43db938b6aaa5688463fe') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c065e132fc54d37c97e43db938b6aaa5688463fe') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '4699f535d2a63653c20467ec52353080178d1e59') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c065e132fc54d37c97e43db938b6aaa5688463fe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') != '823d9cc19c92525deef183cb9c43119c784ca267') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '823d9cc19c92525deef183cb9c43119c784ca267') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '163d4f4febeeae041c3fd1b4c7b34fa2cb94ed07') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '823d9cc19c92525deef183cb9c43119c784ca267') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != 'c0610524fa8082740b49cce3f079aa8ee2123341') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'c0610524fa8082740b49cce3f079aa8ee2123341') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '57132e932249e250c51bf4147f872dd9380a595c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'c0610524fa8082740b49cce3f079aa8ee2123341') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '10c0eb96f936119f2e009062f4a0296e690344e3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '10c0eb96f936119f2e009062f4a0296e690344e3') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '62572f1755d6cb84abe52ee03fc8449aef4df731') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '10c0eb96f936119f2e009062f4a0296e690344e3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== 'b6d8394fd9898242cd1b6f1760e5e4a64f62a424') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '11efd8af718e11ef2d7d62bf04d5d65e4c4150f9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== 'b6d8394fd9898242cd1b6f1760e5e4a64f62a424') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '6a9be9b027fef761e59a84a0df16e922feaf368f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '6a9be9b027fef761e59a84a0df16e922feaf368f') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2f6f66429fb5f59eda2856eb475b6ac2b9246554') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '6a9be9b027fef761e59a84a0df16e922feaf368f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != '2dffbc691beb081b28f91245b809f98e74984f5c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '2dffbc691beb081b28f91245b809f98e74984f5c') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '24baf1891e89b56dfafafcbfb5f5becf2549d837') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '2dffbc691beb081b28f91245b809f98e74984f5c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_23();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '4d8ba0b33d8417fe59d0b9101543e6e5771f8f39') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '4d8ba0b33d8417fe59d0b9101543e6e5771f8f39') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'a032ef53a0995b6dfe723d48a545be6495c4d7f2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '4d8ba0b33d8417fe59d0b9101543e6e5771f8f39') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 366') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
